<script type="text/javascript">
    //签到判断是否手机激活
    function sign_2(){
        $.ajax({
            url :"/?r=member/bdmobile",
            type : "POST",
            dataType : 'json',
            timeout:5000,
            success:function(data) {
                if(data['state']==1){
                    window.location.href="/uc/account"
                }else{
                    sign();
                }
            }
        })

    }


    function score_cad_anim(num){
        var fl_scorenum=$(".fl_scorenum"),td=$(".calendard_td");
        fl_scorenum.css("display","block");
        fl_scorenum.text("+"+num+"积分");
        fl_scorenum.animate({"marginTop":"-20px","opacity":"0"},600,function(){
            fl_scorenum.css("display","none");
        })
        td.append("<var></var>");
    }

    function sign(){
        if( !__loginstate ) {location.href='/?r=member/login'; return;}
        if( !ajaxprocess ) return; ajaxprocess = false;
        $.ajax({
            url:"/?r=score/sign",
            type:"POST",
            data:"",
            dataType:"json",
            timeout:4000,
            success:function(data){
                var re = data.result;
                if( re==1 ){
                    return;
                }else if( re==5 ){
                   return;
                }else if( re==4 ){
                    html_notice = '<span style="width: 240px; height: 20px; float: left;">恭喜您获得'+ ( data.score ) +'个积分</span><span style=" float: left;line-height: 18px;  font-weight:normal;width:240px;height:46px; margin-top: 5px;  margin-left:5px; font-size:12px;">您已连续签到'+ ( data.days ) +'天或'+ ( data.days ) +'天以上，明天签到获得'+ ( data.nextscore ) +'积分</span>';
                    sgin_word = '您已连续签到'+ ( data.days ) +'天或'+ ( data.nextscore ) +'天以上，明天签到获得'+ ( data.nextscore ) +'积分';
                }
                //
                var user_ownscore = document.getElementById('user_ownscore');
                var user_owndays = document.getElementById('user_owndays');
                var user_n_word = document.getElementById('user_n_word');
                var sign_days = parseInt(user_owndays.innerHTML);

                //var tomorrowscore = document.getElementById('tomorrowscore');
                var score = parseInt(user_ownscore.innerHTML);
                //var tscore = parseInt(tomorrowscore.innerHTML);
                var html_notice = '';
                var sgin_word = '';

                score = score + data.score;
                tscore = data.nextscore;
                if( html_notice == '' )
                    html_notice = '<span style="width: 240px; height: 20px; float: left;">恭喜您获得' + ( data.score ) + '个积分</span><span style=" float: left;line-height: 18px; margin-left:5px; margin-top: 5px;  font-weight:normal;width:240px;height:46px; font-size:12px;">您已连续签到'+ ( data.days ) +'天，明天签到获得'+ ( data.nextscore ) +'积分</span>';
                if( sgin_word == '' )
                    sgin_word = '您已连续签到'+ ( data.days ) +'天，明天签到获得'+ ( data.nextscore ) +'积分';
                $('.bannerasgin').html('已签到')


                user_ownscore.innerHTML = score;
                if( document.getElementById('user_ownscore2')){
                    document.getElementById('user_ownscore2').innerHTML = score;
                }

                user_owndays.innerHTML = sign_days+1;
                if( document.getElementById('user_owndays2')){
                    document.getElementById('user_owndays2').innerHTML = sign_days+1;
                }

                user_n_word.innerHTML = "明日可领<strong>"+data.nextscore+"</strong>积分";
                if(  document.getElementById('user_n_word2')){
                    document.getElementById('user_n_word2').innerHTML = "明日可领<em>"+data.nextscore+"</em>积分";
                }

                 $(".calendard_td").parent("span").addClass("cur");
                //tomorrowscore.innerHTML = tscore;
                if( typeof( interfaceSign ) == 'function' )
                    interfaceSign( data );
                else
                    score_cad_anim(data.score);

                var oSginword = document.getElementById("sgin_word");
                if( oSginword ) oSginword.innerHTML = sgin_word;

                var oSign1a = document.getElementById("sign_1_a");
                var oSign2a = document.getElementById("sign_2_a");
                var oSign3a = document.getElementById("sign_3_a");
                var oSign4a = document.getElementById("sign_4_a");
                if( oSign1a ) oSign1a.style.display='none';
                if( oSign2a ) oSign2a.style.display='none';
                if( oSign3a ) oSign3a.style.display='none';
                if( oSign4a ) oSign4a.style.display='none';

                var oSign1b = document.getElementById("sign_1_b");
                var oSign2b = document.getElementById("sign_2_b");
                var oSign3b = document.getElementById("sign_3_b");
                var oSign4b = document.getElementById("sign_4_b");
                if( oSign1b ) oSign1b.style.display='block';
                if( oSign2b ) oSign2b.style.display='block';
                if( oSign3b ) oSign3b.style.display='block';
                if( oSign4b ) oSign4b.style.display='block';

                var credit2 = document.getElementById('credit2');
                if( credit2 ) credit2.innerHTML = score;

                var sign_a = $('.sign_calendar a.sign_btn');
                if( sign_a[0] ){
                    if( sign_a.hasClass('sign0') ) sign_a.removeClass('sign0').addClass('sign1');
                }

                var btn_a = $('.r_fixsign a.btn');
                if( btn_a[0] ){
                    if( btn_a.hasClass('btn0') ) btn_a.removeClass('btn0').addClass('btn1');
                }
                var not_sign = $('.not_sign');
                var has_sign = $('.has_sign');
                var a2 = $('.sc_fix_r a.a2');
                if( not_sign[0] ){
                    a2.addClass('a2_sign');
                    not_sign.css('display', 'none');
                    has_sign.css('display', 'block');
                }

                var is_sign = $('a.is_sign_b0');
                if( is_sign[0] ) {
                    $('a.is_sign_a0').css('display', 'none');
                    is_sign.css('display', 'block');
                }

                var sign1212 = document.getElementById("is_sign_ct");
                if( sign1212 ) {
                    $(sign1212).removeClass('btn0');
                    $(sign1212).addClass('btn1');
                }

            }

        })
    }
</script>
